### [ Return all cases that have a hospitalization of more than 1 day. ]
Answer:
```
{
    ""query"": {
        ""range"": {
            ""HOSPDAYS"": {
                ""gt"": 1
            }
        }
    }
}
```

            ""HOSPDAYS"": {
                ""lt"": 1
            }
        }
    }
}
```

### [On 04/28/2022, how many people have been recorded who are female?]
Answer:
```
{
    ""query"": {
        ""bool"": {
            ""must"": [
                {""match"": {""RECVDATE"": ""04/28/2022""}},
                {""match"": {""SEX"": ""Female""}}
            ]
        }
    },
    ""_source"": [""VAERS_ID""]
}
```
